<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мурлыкать.html>мурлы́кать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">murlýkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to purr</li>

***мусолить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мусолить.html>мусо́лить</a> (30328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мусолить.html>мусо́лить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">musólitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замусолить.html>замусо́лить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">намусо́лить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wet with saliva</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to leave dirty marks on with dirty or sticky fingers</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend too much time (over); to discuss or to speak about over and over again</li></ol>

***мусор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мусор.html>му́сор</a> (3764)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мусор.html>му́сор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">músor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мусор.html>му́сора</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>garbage, debris, refuse</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отброс.html>отбро́с</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otbrós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отход.html>отхо́ды</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otxódy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сор.html>сор</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлам.html>хлам</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xlam</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the pre-1917 acronym <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мус.html>Мус́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">MUS</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:московский.html>моско́вский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголовный.html>уголо́вный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыск.html>сыск</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Moskóvskij ugolóvnyj sysk</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moscow_Criminal_Investigations_Department" class="extiw" title="w:Moscow Criminal Investigations Department">Moscow Criminal Detective Department</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мусор.html>му́сор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">músor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мусор.html>му́сора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мусор.html>мусора́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мусор.html>мусоро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cop, pig <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">policeman</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">cop, pejorative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мент.html>мент</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ment</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:легавый.html>лега́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">legávyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фараон.html>фарао́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">faraón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мусульманин.html>мусульма́нин</a> (12336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">мөселман</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">möselman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">мұсылман</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">musılman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)  + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ин</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-in</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***мутить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́ть</a> (12572)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mǫtiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stir, trouble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замутить.html>замути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make (water) muddy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мути́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mutítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">замути́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamutítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">помути́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cloud (the mind), to dull (the senses)</li>
<li>to incite to rebel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be nauseated
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>mutít</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is nauseated</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мути́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mutítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помутиться.html>помути́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pomutítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_3">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">взму́чивать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vzmúčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муть.html>муть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мутный.html>му́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mútnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мутне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:мутнеть.html>мутне́й</a></b>)

***муха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a> (1648)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*muxa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mows-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mus-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mew-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">múxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fly <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">insect</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>дохнут</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>múxi</b> doxnut</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you could die of boredom</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ pod múxoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be mellow; be tight; be under the sauce</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> мёд</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak múxi na mjód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">like wasps around jam</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слон.html>слона́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">délatʹ iz múxi sloná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">make a mountain out of a molehill</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сонный.html>со́нная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak sónnaja múxa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">like a sleepy fly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>кака́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:укусить.html>укуси́ла</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kakaja <b>múxa</b> jevó ukusíla?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what's got into him?; what's bitten him?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лых</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do bélyx <b>mux</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">till snow falls</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обидеть.html>оби́дит</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on i <b>múxi</b> ne obídit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he wouldn't hurt a fly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слышно.html>слы́шно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́ха</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пролететь.html>пролети́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">slýšno, kak <b>múxa</b> proletít</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one could hear a pin drop</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:считать.html>счита́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sčitátʹ <b>mux</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to gape</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мереть.html>мру́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:муха.html>му́хи</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní mrut kak <b>múxi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">they drop like flies</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мухобо́йка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">muxobójka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мучение.html>муче́ние</a> (8483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
